        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





Hi Team. In windows .lnk, .local, .url files are considered to be shortcut and sensitive extension also it is renamed to .download by default in chrome. But i have found a way to download the .lnk file



<span class="line"><!---->Hi Team. In windows .lnk, .local, .url files are considered to be shortcut and sensitive extension also it is renamed to .download by default in chrome. But i have found a way to download the .lnk file<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Ref: 



<span class="line"><!---->Ref: <!----></span>





https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1140417



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1140417"><!---->https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1140417<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





Found a alternate way via chrome.fileSystem.chooseEntry (Chrome API)



<span class="line"><!---->Found a alternate way via chrome.fileSystem.chooseEntry (Chrome API)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





FYI: tested in latest Version of chrome



<span class="line"><!---->FYI: tested in latest Version of chrome<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Check Reproduce Steps



<span class="line"><!---->Check Reproduce Steps<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: Version 108.0.5359.125 (Official Build) (64-bit)



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: Version 108.0.5359.125 (Official Build) (64-bit)<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows 10 (with Latest Patch)



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows 10 (with Latest Patch)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. Download the Below Files and add it as Extension to the chrome



<span class="line"><!---->1. Download the Below Files and add it as Extension to the chrome<!----></span>



<br>





2. After added, it popus a index page, Hold enter for a second.



<span class="line"><!---->2. After added, it popus a index page, Hold enter for a second.<!----></span>



<br>





3. You can find .lnk file saved in the Download Directory



<span class="line"><!---->3. You can find .lnk file saved in the Download Directory<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Which is restricted by default. Tested for .local too



<span class="line"><!---->Which is restricted by default. Tested for .local too<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->),<!----></span>





 which are long deprecated (

).



<span class="line"><!---->).<!----></span>





 "Chrome Apps support on Windows/macOS/Linux ending for everyone" appears to have happened last August (



<span class="line"><!----> "Chrome Apps support on Windows/macOS/Linux ending for everyone" appears to have happened last August (<!----></span>

Since this requires an API restricted to platform apps and platform apps can only be installed locally unpacked, this falls outside the threat model for extensions. See: 



<span class="line"><!---->Since this requires an API restricted to platform apps and platform apps can only be installed locally unpacked, this falls outside the threat model for extensions. See: <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/HEAD/extensions/docs/security_faq.md#What-is-our-stance-on-unpacked-extensions



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/HEAD/extensions/docs/security_faq.md#What-is-our-stance-on-unpacked-extensions"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/HEAD/extensions/docs/security_faq.md#What-is-our-stance-on-unpacked-extensions<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





Due to this I'm marking this wont fix for now, but if you can identify another way to trigger this which doesn't require a user to load an unpacked extension feel free to reopen.



<span class="line"><!---->Due to this I'm marking this wont fix for now, but if you can identify another way to trigger this which doesn't require a user to load an unpacked extension feel free to reopen.<!----></span>

Ah right, sorry about that. I was more meaning that the chrome.fileSystem.chooseEntry API itself is restricted to only be available to platform apps and new platforms apps cannot be uploaded to the Webstore, so any new legitimate extension would not be able to use this to attack a victim.



<span class="line"><!---->Ah right, sorry about that. I was more meaning that the chrome.fileSystem.chooseEntry API itself is restricted to only be available to platform apps and new platforms apps cannot be uploaded to the Webstore, so any new legitimate extension would not be able to use this to attack a victim.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





However discussing this a bit more in person, there is still the possibility of an EXISTING app on the Webstore updating to take advantage of this so it would be exploitable that way.



<span class="line"><!---->However discussing this a bit more in person, there is still the possibility of an EXISTING app on the Webstore updating to take advantage of this so it would be exploitable that way.<!----></span>



<br>

I'd like to start by clarifying a couple of points about this ticket:



<span class="line"><!---->I'd like to start by clarifying a couple of points about this ticket:<!----></span>



<br>





- fileSystem.chooseEntry is NOT available to Chrome Extensions in general, as can be seen in [1].



<span class="line"><!---->- fileSystem.chooseEntry is NOT available to Chrome Extensions in general, as can be seen in [1].<!----></span>



<br>





- both "unpacked extensions" provided to repro the issue are actually ChromeApps, as their manifests include the "app.background" key (see [2]).



<span class="line"><!---->- both "unpacked extensions" provided to repro the issue are actually ChromeApps, as their manifests include the "app.background" key (see [2]).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In light of the points above, the only way to exploit this API was identified by tjudkins@ in 



<span class="line"><!---->In light of the points above, the only way to exploit this API was identified by tjudkins@ in <!----></span>





comment#17



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c17"><!---->comment#17<!----></a>





: "an EXISTING app on the Webstore updating to take advantage of this". This is indeed an exploitation path that needs to be discussed further with the security team to assess risks and appropriate mitigations.



<span class="line"><!---->: "an EXISTING app on the Webstore updating to take advantage of this". This is indeed an exploitation path that needs to be discussed further with the security team to assess risks and appropriate mitigations.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>

HI Team. By doing some more analysis i have found that this will lead to leak the user environment variable



<span class="line"><!---->HI Team. By doing some more analysis i have found that this will lead to leak the user environment variable<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





.URL & .LNK files support to load Icon from remote shares via UNC Path. In addition to this windows will resolve the UNC path to map the Environment variable if any



<span class="line"><!---->.URL &amp; .LNK files support to load Icon from remote shares via UNC Path. In addition to this windows will resolve the UNC path to map the Environment variable if any<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For eg: \\<server>\\%USERNAME%.txt



<span class="line"><!---->For eg: \\&lt;server&gt;\\%USERNAME%.txt<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This will be resolved as \\<server>\\ameen.txt and makes a connection to Remote Server.



<span class="line"><!---->This will be resolved as \\&lt;server&gt;\\ameen.txt and makes a connection to Remote Server.<!----></span>



<br>





We can create some rouge SMB Server to parse the Request and get the requested UNC Path to Find the System variable of the victim machine



<span class="line"><!---->We can create some rouge SMB Server to parse the Request and get the requested UNC Path to Find the System variable of the victim machine<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Reference of ENV leak via .url file: 



<span class="line"><!---->Reference of ENV leak via .url file: <!----></span>





https://insert-script.blogspot.com/2018/08/leaking-environment-variables-in_20.html

<span class="line"><!---->Also this Bug is having similar impact to the below Already fixed chromium Bug. Kindly initiate a quick fix on this<!----></span>

After discussing this issue with the Chrome Security team, we reached the conclusion that, while this is indeed a Chrome Apps vulnerability, the risk is very limited by a number of factors:



<span class="line"><!---->After discussing this issue with the Chrome Security team, we reached the conclusion that, while this is indeed a Chrome Apps vulnerability, the risk is very limited by a number of factors:<!----></span>



<br>





- this exploit affects only Windows users



<span class="line"><!---->- this exploit affects only Windows users<!----></span>



<br>





- Chrome Apps will not work on Windows devices starting from M112



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome Apps will not work on Windows devices starting from M112<!----></span>



<br>





- the only way to exploit this is by updating a Chrome App that is already listed in CWS



<span class="line"><!---->- the only way to exploit this is by updating a Chrome App that is already listed in CWS<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For these reasons we are not going to implement a quick fix to block this behaviour and will keep the bug open with a lower priority until M112 is available on stable channel.



<span class="line"><!---->For these reasons we are not going to implement a quick fix to block this behaviour and will keep the bug open with a lower priority until M112 is available on stable channel.<!----></span>

That is fair - the only stopped being launch-able & installable recently. I'm not sure how bounties worked, I'll mark this as "Fixed". The scope of attack is limited here:



<span class="line"><!---->That is fair - the only stopped being launch-able &amp; installable recently. I'm not sure how bounties worked, I'll mark this as "Fixed". The scope of attack is limited here:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





- I'm pretty sure the the 'sideload' version of this attack isn't in scope of our security, I'll leave that for security folks to reason about (as it's a developer thing that requires special install paths that aren't normal for a user). Kinda like asking the user to mess with chrome://flags.



<span class="line"><!---->- I'm pretty sure the the 'sideload' version of this attack isn't in scope of our security, I'll leave that for security folks to reason about (as it's a developer thing that requires special install paths that aren't normal for a user). Kinda like asking the user to mess with chrome://flags.<!----></span>



<br>





- This attack was limited to only existing platform apps in the web store, as new ones couldn't be uploaded.



<span class="line"><!---->- This attack was limited to only existing platform apps in the web store, as new ones couldn't be uploaded.<!----></span>



<br>





- These chrome apps stopped being installable from the chrome web store recently, and they cannot be launched anymore starting m113 (they have had deprecated messaging for the last 6 months or so in product, and we have communicated their deprecation for years).



<span class="line"><!---->- These chrome apps stopped being installable from the chrome web store recently, and they cannot be launched anymore starting m113 (they have had deprecated messaging for the last 6 months or so in product, and we have communicated their deprecation for years).<!----></span>

        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;

          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
